:\r\nThe Fall of the Dungeon Guardians is an RPG Dungeon Crawler game, in First Person View, inspired by classics like Dungeon Master‚Ñ¢ and Might & Magic¬Æ, but featuring a modern combat system based on the triptych ‚Äútank/damage dealer/healer‚Äù mechanism.\r\n\r\nStory :\r\nYou‚Äôre a newly employed guard of a prison deep inside a dungeon. The night of your arrival, strange things happen and when you wake up in the morning, all prisoners have escaped amidst chaos. The warden wisely decides to leave the dungeon as quickly as possible, while tasking you to run after the escaping prisoners. You then assemble your team and venture into the mysterious dungeon.\r\n\r\nA Call For Adventure :\r\nEnter a big, massive dungeon, full of danger, mystery and secrets.\r\nFight your way through hordes of enemies and powerful creatures.\r\nExplore intricate corridors, underground palaces, mines fallen into oblivion and evil crypts.\r\nSolve puzzles, avoid deadly traps, uncover hidden passages, and keep your bearing through mazes & hallways.\r\n\r\nCharacter Building :\r\nYou‚Äôll take command of a party of 4 guardians. Each guardian comes with a set of spells & abilities, with new ones appearing over the course of the adventure.\r\nFor each new level reached, the guardians get a point to use in their talent trees, allowing them to reinforce their abilities or gain new powers.\r\nThere are 4 classes to choose from: the warrior, the healer, the mage & the rogue. Each class has 3 specializations represented by a talent tree, and each specialization comes with its own set of abilities. So you have 12 base build-ups. In addition, your guardians can choose freely to spend their talent points in any of the 3 specializations of their class, allowing for even more varied set-ups.\r\n\r\nThe dungeon is filled with loot: epic armors, legendary weapons and mystical, magical items. Often when you kill a group of enemies, they‚Äôll drop a random piece of equipment that one of your guardians can use, raising more and more of their powers.\r\n\r\nEvolved Combat System :\r\nThe combat is focused on the triptych ‚Äútank/damage dealer/healer‚Äù mechanism, coupled with an exciting threat mechanism: your healer‚Äôs spells directly threaten all the enemies nearby, and thus your tank must use his abilities to attract their wrath and protect the healer. The tank must then be able to mitigate a lot of the enemy damage using his defensive skills.\r\nYour last 2 guardians will be the damage dealers, trying to kill the enemies as fast as possible, while they‚Äôre busy with the tank.\r\nAll guardians get a lot of abilities and not only will using the right one at the right moment be essential to your party‚Äôs survival, but also combining different abilities in sequence to maximize their efficiency will be required to vanquish your strongest foes.\r\nIt sounds like a lot, but fortunately the game comes with an active pause: you can pause the game whenever you feel like it, check everything, queue the next abilities for your guardians, and then resume the game.\r\n\r\nYou don‚Äôt like tanks, or you don‚Äôt like pausing the game? No problem, just lower the game difficulty, and you‚Äôll be able to play without a real tank or pausing. You can precisely tune the difficulty at any time during your exploration.\r\n\r\nUnlike old-school FPV Dungeon Crawlers, you don‚Äôt have to strafe-turn-strafe-turn all the time in Dungeon Guardians. Your tank comes with serious defensive skills (armor, dodge & parry) that let him handle most of the enemy attacks, as long as the healer backs him up. So most fights are done while standing your ground.\r\nHowever, occasionally your whole party will have to dodge some extremely powerful enemy attacks, usually by walking back, so you‚Äôll still need some moving reflexes and awareness of your surroundings during the fights.\r\n\r\nBuilt-in Map editor & Modding :\r\nThe game comes with a full featured map editor, letting you create your own dungeons. The basics are very simple, but a bit of learning will be required to handle the more advanced puzzle mechanisms.\r\nAdditionally, with the Modding SDK, you‚Äôll be able to fine-tune the existing enemies, classes, specializations, abilities, talents, gear, and enchantments, and with a bit of dedication you should be able to add your own, and even add sound FX or music.\r\n\r\nGame Features :\r\n    - 4-character Party\r\n    - Grid-based movement : your party moves 1 square at the time, and turns by a quarter\r\n    - First person view\r\n    - 4 classes, 12 specializations\r\n    - 5 playable races : human, dwarf, elf, dark elf, halfling\r\n    - Active pause (ie: you can pause the game and still queue commands for your party members), and numerous optional auto-pauses\r\n    - 25-50 hours of gameplay, depending on your own skills and the difficulty settings\r\n    - 20 bosses\r\n    - 100 kinds of creatures (including variations)\r\n    - Puzzles (the few ones required to finish the game are easy to solve)\r\n    - A lot of tactical combat\r\n    - Built-in Map Editor & Modding support \r\n\r\nReviews :\r\n‚ÄúThe combat is exquisitely balanced. Yes, it relies on the generic trio of a tank to absorb enemy attacks, a healer to keep the tank standing, and two damage-dealers to take out the actual enemies. Yes, that‚Äôs a bit of an unexpected approach for a game that‚Äôs so old school in every other aspect.
